    //一些通用的页面和插件控制
    function InitCommonControl() {
        if (document.getElementById("calendar")) {
            //点击除日期按钮和日期选择框外的任意地方都关闭日期框
            document.getElementById("calendar").onclick = function (ev) { ev = ev || window.event; ev.cancelBubble = true; }
            if (document.getElementById("calendarBtn")) document.getElementById("calendarBtn").onclick = function (ev) { ev = ev || window.event; ev.cancelBubble = true; MM_showHideLayers('Layer2', '', 'show'); }
            document.documentElement.onclick = function (ev) { MM_showHideLayers('Layer2', '', 'hidden'); }
        }
    }
    SyncDarkCheck();
    InitCommonControl();
</script>
